# Echoes of the Dawnforge — Complete Sublocation Special Event Catalog
These optional special events trigger only after the player reaches the listed required level. They grant **no XP**; all rewards are unique loot, relic patterns, cosmetics, materials, or encounter trophies. Each monster is a raised variant of a monster or boss family from `World.txt`.

## The Urban Sprawl

### SEV-001 — Overcharged Incident: Spire-Foot Transit Plaza
- **Sublocation:** Spire-Foot Transit Plaza
- **Required player level:** 20
- **Recommended combat rating:** 22
- **Event type:** Elite Ambush / Boss-Echo
- **XP reward:** 0 completion XP; 0 spawned-enemy XP
- **Trigger:** Trigger only when player level >= 20, player enters or completes a combat action inside Spire-Foot Transit Plaza, and the sublocation has not awarded its weekly unique-loot eligibility. Completion XP and spawned-enemy XP are both forcibly set to 0.
- **Encounter goal:** Break the Null Anomaly echo before its signature phase mechanic fully resolves, while suppressing support variants and maintaining encounter control.
- **Hazard profile:** high-speed transit sweeps, lane swaps, and lethal timing windows
- **Empowered mechanic:** Overcharged Echo Rule: the boss repeats one signature world mechanic at 70%, 40%, and 15% health, each time with a tighter counter window.
- **Failure state:** Event fails if the local anomaly reaches 100% intensity, all eligible players are downed, or the primary variant completes its empowered phase three times. Failure gives no XP and no loot roll.
- **Unique loot:** Spire-Foot Null Ring — Refined Relic ring, item power 540
- **Loot rule:** Guaranteed first-clear: Spire-Foot Null Ring pattern token + Refined Relic crafting imprint. Repeat clear: 20% chance for the unique ring; pity token after 8 eligible clears.
- **Unique perk:** Unique Perk: while inside Urban-type arenas, gain a short defensive or traversal proc after countering Null Anomaly mechanics. Does not increase XP gain.
- **Group scaling:** Solo-scaled, 2-player, 4-player, and 8-player public-event variants; HP scales by +65% per additional player after the first, damage scales by +8% per additional player, and loot eligibility requires active contribution.

**Raised monster stat block:**

| Variant | Role | Standard Level | Event Level | HP | Damage | Armor | Shield | Stagger Res. | Speed | XP | Mechanic Basis |
|---|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---|
| Overcharged Null Anomaly | Primary Variant / Event Anchor | 20 | 22 | 25752 | 736 | 43 | 107 | 129 | 1.15 | 0 | Echo Splintering; Gravity Reversal |
| Overcharged Iron-Jaw Hound | Support Variant 1 | 13 | 22 | 3024 | 187 | 49 | 0 | 57 | 1.35 | 0 | Latch; teammate vault-kick assist |
| Overcharged Tremor-Fiend | Support Variant 2 | 18 | 22 | 3558 | 204 | 55 | 0 | 90 | 0.81 | 0 | Metronome Strike; Sonic Bellow |

### SEV-002 — Bark-Crowned Incident: Lower Civic Ring
- **Sublocation:** Lower Civic Ring
- **Required player level:** 20
- **Recommended combat rating:** 22
- **Event type:** Environmental Surge / Elite-Variant
- **XP reward:** 0 completion XP; 0 spawned-enemy XP
- **Trigger:** Trigger only when player level >= 20, player enters or completes a combat action inside Lower Civic Ring, and the sublocation has not awarded its weekly unique-loot eligibility. Completion XP and spawned-enemy XP are both forcibly set to 0.
- **Encounter goal:** Hunt the mobile flanker variant, protect isolated players from pin mechanics, and force the enemy into a punishable arena state.
- **Hazard profile:** elite spawn pressure, sublocation-specific chokepoints, and forced traversal interrupts
- **Empowered mechanic:** Bark-Crowned Pack Latch: if the first latch is not broken within 4 seconds, a support hound joins and halves the victim’s healing received.
- **Failure state:** Event fails if the local anomaly reaches 100% intensity, all eligible players are downed, or the primary variant completes its empowered phase three times. Failure gives no XP and no loot roll.
- **Unique loot:** Lower Iron-Jaw Amulet — Refined Relic amulet, item power 547
- **Loot rule:** Guaranteed first-clear: Lower Iron-Jaw Amulet pattern token + Refined Relic crafting imprint. Repeat clear: 20% chance for the unique amulet; pity token after 8 eligible clears.
- **Unique perk:** Unique Perk: while inside Urban-type arenas, gain a short defensive or traversal proc after countering Iron-Jaw Hound mechanics. Does not increase XP gain.
- **Group scaling:** Solo-scaled, 2-player, 4-player, and 8-player public-event variants; HP scales by +65% per additional player after the first, damage scales by +8% per additional player, and loot eligibility requires active contribution.

**Raised monster stat block:**

| Variant | Role | Standard Level | Event Level | HP | Damage | Armor | Shield | Stagger Res. | Speed | XP | Mechanic Basis |
|---|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---|
| Bark-Crowned Iron-Jaw Hound | Primary Variant / Event Anchor | 13 | 22 | 3024 | 187 | 49 | 0 | 57 | 1.35 | 0 | Latch; teammate vault-kick assist |
| Bark-Crowned Tremor-Fiend | Support Variant 1 | 18 | 22 | 3558 | 204 | 55 | 0 | 90 | 0.81 | 0 | Metronome Strike; Sonic Bellow |
| Bark-Crowned Venom-Spitter | Support Variant 2 | 15 | 22 | 1842 | 139 | 23 | 0 | 31 | 1.13 | 0 | Telegraphed Projectiles; Projectile Reversal |

### SEV-003 — Echo-Split Incident: Collapsed Skywalk Lanes
- **Sublocation:** Collapsed Skywalk Lanes
- **Required player level:** 20
- **Recommended combat rating:** 22
- **Event type:** Variant Hunt / Elite-Variant
- **XP reward:** 0 completion XP; 0 spawned-enemy XP
- **Trigger:** Trigger only when player level >= 20, player enters or completes a combat action inside Collapsed Skywalk Lanes, and the sublocation has not awarded its weekly unique-loot eligibility. Completion XP and spawned-enemy XP are both forcibly set to 0.
- **Encounter goal:** Control priority targets, solve the counter/vault pattern under added hazard pressure, and collapse the elite formation without dropping flow.
- **Hazard profile:** elite spawn pressure, sublocation-specific chokepoints, and forced traversal interrupts
- **Empowered mechanic:** Echo-Split Corrosive Ricochet: reversed projectiles split once, rewarding precise counters but punishing mistimed reversal spam.
- **Failure state:** Event fails if the local anomaly reaches 100% intensity, all eligible players are downed, or the primary variant completes its empowered phase three times. Failure gives no XP and no loot roll.
- **Unique loot:** Collapsed Venom-Spitter Main-Hand Weapon — Refined Relic main-hand weapon, item power 554
- **Loot rule:** Guaranteed first-clear: Collapsed Venom-Spitter Main-Hand Weapon pattern token + Refined Relic crafting imprint. Repeat clear: 20% chance for the unique main-hand weapon; pity token after 8 eligible clears.
- **Unique perk:** Unique Perk: while inside Urban-type arenas, gain a short defensive or traversal proc after countering Venom-Spitter mechanics. Does not increase XP gain.
- **Group scaling:** Solo-scaled, 2-player, 4-player, and 8-player public-event variants; HP scales by +65% per additional player after the first, damage scales by +8% per additional player, and loot eligibility requires active contribution.

| Echo-Split Aegis Carapace | Support Variant 1 | 12 | 22 | 3852 | 162 | 93 | 81 | 76 | 0.86 | 0 | Frontal Deflection; Vault-Over Vulnerability |
| Echo-Split Tremor-Fiend | Support Variant 2 | 18 | 22 | 3558 | 204 | 55 | 0 | 90 | 0.81 | 0 | Metronome Strike; Sonic Bellow |

### SEV-004 — Null-Branded Incident: Alliance Muster Square
- **Sublocation:** Alliance Muster Square
- **Required player level:** 20
- **Recommended combat rating:** 22
- **Event type:** Timed Defense / Elite-Variant
- **XP reward:** 0 completion XP; 0 spawned-enemy XP
- **Trigger:** Trigger only when player level >= 20, player enters or completes a combat action inside Alliance Muster Square, and the sublocation has not awarded its weekly unique-loot eligibility. Completion XP and spawned-enemy XP are both forcibly set to 0.
- **Encounter goal:** Control priority targets, solve the counter/vault pattern under added hazard pressure, and collapse the elite formation without dropping flow.
- **Hazard profile:** elite spawn pressure, sublocation-specific chokepoints, and forced traversal interrupts
- **Empowered mechanic:** Null-Branded Syncopation: Metronome Strike intentionally skips every fourth beat, punishing players who rely only on memorized rhythm.
- **Failure state:** Event fails if the local anomaly reaches 100% intensity, all eligible players are downed, or the primary variant completes its empowered phase three times. Failure gives no XP and no loot roll.
- **Unique loot:** Alliance Tremor-Fiend Off-Hand Focus — Refined Relic off-hand focus, item power 561
- **Loot rule:** Guaranteed first-clear: Alliance Tremor-Fiend Off-Hand Focus pattern token + Refined Relic crafting imprint. Repeat clear: 20% chance for the unique off-hand focus; pity token after 8 eligible clears.
- **Unique perk:** Unique Perk: while inside Urban-type arenas, gain a short defensive or traversal proc after countering Tremor-Fiend mechanics. Does not increase XP gain.
- **Group scaling:** Solo-scaled, 2-player, 4-player, and 8-player public-event variants; HP scales by +65% per additional player after the first, damage scales by +8% per additional player, and loot eligibility requires active contribution.

## The Zenith Spire

### SEV-006 — Grav-Torn Incident: Glass Lobby Atrium

- **Required player level:** 20
- **Recommended combat rating:** 22
- **Event type:** Horde Compression / Elite-Variant
- **XP reward:** 0 completion XP; 0 spawned-enemy XP
- **Trigger:** Trigger only when player level >= 20, player enters or completes a combat action inside Glass Lobby Atrium, and the sublocation has not awarded its weekly unique-loot eligibility. Completion XP and spawned-enemy XP are both forcibly set to 0.
- **Encounter goal:** Survive a condensed horde pattern, prevent escalation loops, and eliminate the Iron-Jaw Hound variant commander before it converts the sublocation into a permanent hazard node.
- **Hazard profile:** elite spawn pressure, sublocation-specific chokepoints, and forced traversal interrupts
- **Empowered mechanic:** Grav-Torn Pack Latch: if the first latch is not broken within 4 seconds, a support hound joins and halves the victim’s healing received.
- **Failure state:** Event fails if the local anomaly reaches 100% intensity, all eligible players are downed, or the primary variant completes its empowered phase three times. Failure gives no XP and no loot roll.

- **Loot rule:** Guaranteed first-clear: Glass Iron-Jaw Class Mod pattern token + Refined Relic crafting imprint. Repeat clear: 20% chance for the unique class mod; pity token after 8 eligible clears.

- **Group scaling:** Solo-scaled, 2-player, 4-player, and 8-player public-event variants; HP scales by +65% per additional player after the first, damage scales by +8% per additional player, and loot eligibility requires active contribution.

### SEV-012 — Ash-Baptized Incident: Broken Ventilation Spine
- **Sublocation:** Broken Ventilation Spine

- **Recommended combat rating:** 23
- **Event type:** Environmental Surge / Elite-Variant
- **XP reward:** 0 completion XP; 0 spawned-enemy XP

- **Encounter goal:** Control priority targets, solve the counter/vault pattern under added hazard pressure, and collapse the elite formation without dropping flow.
- **Hazard profile:** elite spawn pressure, sublocation-specific chokepoints, and forced traversal interrupts

### SEV-024 — Grav-Torn Incident: Wall-Run Market Roofs
- **Sublocation:** Wall-Run Market Roofs
- **Required player level:** 22
- **Recommended combat rating:** 24
- **Event type:** Timed Defense / Elite-Variant
- **XP reward:** 0 completion XP; 0 spawned-enemy XP
- **Trigger:** Trigger only when player level >= 22, player enters or completes a combat action inside Wall-Run Market Roofs, and the sublocation has not awarded its weekly unique-loot eligibility. Completion XP and spawned-enemy XP are both forcibly set to 0.
- **Encounter goal:** Control priority targets, solve the counter/vault pattern under added hazard pressure, and collapse the elite formation without dropping flow.
- **Hazard profile:** high-speed transit sweeps, lane swaps, and lethal timing windows
- **Empowered mechanic:** Grav-Torn Syncopation: Metronome Strike intentionally skips every fourth beat, punishing players who rely only on memorized rhythm.
- **Failure state:** Event fails if the local anomaly reaches 100% intensity, all eligible players are downed, or the primary variant completes its empowered phase three times. Failure gives no XP and no loot roll.
- **Unique loot:** Wall-Run Tremor-Fiend Helmet — Refined Relic helmet, item power 597
- **Loot rule:** Guaranteed first-clear: Wall-Run Tremor-Fiend Helmet pattern token + Refined Relic crafting imprint. Repeat clear: 20% chance for the unique helmet; pity token after 8 eligible clears.
- **Unique perk:** Unique Perk: while inside Provisioning-type arenas, gain a short defensive or traversal proc after countering Tremor-Fiend mechanics. Does not increase XP gain.
- **Group scaling:** Solo-scaled, 2-player, 4-player, and 8-player public-event variants; HP scales by +65% per additional player after the first, damage scales by +8% per additional player, and loot eligibility requires active contribution.

**Raised monster stat block:**

| Variant | Role | Standard Level | Event Level | HP | Damage | Armor | Shield | Stagger Res. | Speed | XP | Mechanic Basis |
|---|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---|
| Grav-Torn Tremor-Fiend | Primary Variant / Event Anchor | 18 | 24 | 4305 | 238 | 59 | 0 | 96 | 0.81 | 0 | Metronome Strike; Sonic Bellow |

- **Recommended combat rating:** 24

- **Encounter goal:** Survive a condensed horde pattern, prevent escalation loops, and eliminate the Scrap-Phalanx variant commander before it converts the sublocation into a permanent hazard node.
- **Hazard profile:** high-speed transit sweeps, lane swaps, and lethal timing windows
- **Empowered mechanic:** Ablative Collapsing Shell: dive-bombing the phalanx breaks the shield but creates shrapnel lanes that must be vaulted.
- **Failure state:** Event fails if the local anomaly reaches 100% intensity, all eligible players are downed, or the primary variant completes its empowered phase three times. Failure gives no XP and no loot roll.
- **Unique loot:** Vendor Scrap-Phalanx Chest Armor — Refined Relic chest armor, item power 604
- **Loot rule:** Guaranteed first-clear: Vendor Scrap-Phalanx Chest Armor pattern token + Refined Relic crafting imprint. Repeat clear: 20% chance for the unique chest armor; pity token after 8 eligible clears.
- **Unique perk:** Unique Perk: while inside Provisioning-type arenas, gain a short defensive or traversal proc after countering Scrap-Phalanx mechanics. Does not increase XP gain.
- **Group scaling:** Solo-scaled, 2-player, 4-player, and 8-player public-event variants; HP scales by +65% per additional player after the first, damage scales by +8% per additional player, and loot eligibility requires active contribution.

- **XP reward:** 0 completion XP; 0 spawned-enemy XP
- **Trigger:** Trigger only when player level >= 23, player enters or completes a combat action inside Service Vehicle Depot, and the sublocation has not awarded its weekly unique-loot eligibility. Completion XP and spawned-enemy XP are both forcibly set to 0.
- **Encounter goal:** Hunt the mobile flanker variant, protect isolated players from pin mechanics, and force the enemy into a punishable arena state.
- **Hazard profile:** high-speed transit sweeps, lane swaps, and lethal timing windows
- **Empowered mechanic:** Spore-Sick Pack Latch: if the first latch is not broken within 4 seconds, a support hound joins and halves the victim’s healing received.
- **Failure state:** Event fails if the local anomaly reaches 100% intensity, all eligible players are downed, or the primary variant completes its empowered phase three times. Failure gives no XP and no loot roll.
- **Unique loot:** Service Iron-Jaw Weapon Skin — Refined Relic weapon skin, item power 622
- **Loot rule:** Guaranteed first-clear: Service Iron-Jaw Weapon Skin pattern token + Refined Relic crafting imprint. Repeat clear: 20% chance for the unique weapon skin; pity token after 8 eligible clears.
- **Unique perk:** Unique Perk: while inside On-Demand-type arenas, gain a short defensive or traversal proc after countering Iron-Jaw Hound mechanics. Does not increase XP gain.
- **Group scaling:** Solo-scaled, 2-player, 4-player, and 8-player public-event variants; HP scales by +65% per additional player after the first, damage scales by +8% per additional player, and loot eligibility requires active contribution.

- **Encounter goal:** Break the Null Anomaly echo before its signature phase mechanic fully resolves, while suppressing support variants and maintaining encounter control.
- **Hazard profile:** reverting geometry, data-laser sweeps, and UI-noise distraction hazards
- **Empowered mechanic:** Chrome-Maw Echo Rule: the boss repeats one signature world mechanic at 70%, 40%, and 15% health, each time with a tighter counter window.
- **Failure state:** Event fails if the local anomaly reaches 100% intensity, all eligible players are downed, or the primary variant completes its empowered phase three times. Failure gives no XP and no loot roll.

- **Loot rule:** Guaranteed first-clear: Slot-Lantern Null Back Trophy pattern token + Refined Relic crafting imprint. Repeat clear: 20% chance for the unique back trophy; pity token after 8 eligible clears.

- **Group scaling:** Solo-scaled, 2-player, 4-player, and 8-player public-event variants; HP scales by +65% per additional player after the first, damage scales by +8% per additional player, and loot eligibility requires active contribution.

### SEV-047 — Sovereign-Touched Incident: Poacher-Drone Blind
- **Sublocation:** Poacher-Drone Blind
- **Required player level:** 24
- **Recommended combat rating:** 26
- **Event type:** Mini-Boss Echo / Elite-Variant
- **XP reward:** 0 completion XP; 0 spawned-enemy XP
- **Trigger:** Trigger only when player level >= 24, player enters or completes a combat action inside Poacher-Drone Blind, and the sublocation has not awarded its weekly unique-loot eligibility. Completion XP and spawned-enemy XP are both forcibly set to 0.
- **Encounter goal:** Defeat the raised Siphon-Ticks variant and cleanse the triggered anomaly without allowing the mechanic stack to reach maximum intensity.
- **Hazard profile:** root snares, moving beast-platforms, and canopy traversal pressure
- **Empowered mechanic:** Sovereign-Touched Deep Siphon: stolen meter decays every second until the fleeing tick is killed; recovery requires a chase route through Poacher-Drone Blind.
- **Failure state:** Event fails if the local anomaly reaches 100% intensity, all eligible players are downed, or the primary variant completes its empowered phase three times. Failure gives no XP and no loot roll.
- **Unique loot:** Poacher-Drone Siphon-Ticks Class Mod — Refined Relic class mod, item power 619
- **Loot rule:** Guaranteed first-clear: Poacher-Drone Siphon-Ticks Class Mod pattern token + Refined Relic crafting imprint. Repeat clear: 20% chance for the unique class mod; pity token after 8 eligible clears.
- **Unique perk:** Unique Perk: while inside Pachyderm-type arenas, gain a short defensive or traversal proc after countering Siphon-Ticks mechanics. Does not increase XP gain.
- **Group scaling:** Solo-scaled, 2-player, 4-player, and 8-player public-event variants; HP scales by +65% per additional player after the first, damage scales by +8% per additional player, and loot eligibility requires active contribution.

**Raised monster stat block:**

- **Trigger:** Trigger only when player level >= 25, player enters or completes a combat action inside Silent Pool, and the sublocation has not awarded its weekly unique-loot eligibility. Completion XP and spawned-enemy XP are both forcibly set to 0.
- **Encounter goal:** Control priority targets, solve the counter/vault pattern under added hazard pressure, and collapse the elite formation without dropping flow.
- **Hazard profile:** tempo-locked shockwaves, parry-window distortion, and bass pulses that punish dropped combos
- **Empowered mechanic:** Echo-Split Syncopation: Metronome Strike intentionally skips every fourth beat, punishing players who rely only on memorized rhythm.
- **Failure state:** Event fails if the local anomaly reaches 100% intensity, all eligible players are downed, or the primary variant completes its empowered phase three times. Failure gives no XP and no loot roll.
- **Unique loot:** Silent Tremor-Fiend Main-Hand Weapon — Epic Relic main-hand weapon, item power 644
- **Loot rule:** Guaranteed first-clear: Silent Tremor-Fiend Main-Hand Weapon pattern token + Epic Relic crafting imprint. Repeat clear: 16% chance for the unique main-hand weapon; pity token after 8 eligible clears.
- **Unique perk:** Unique Perk: while inside Whispering-type arenas, gain a short defensive or traversal proc after countering Tremor-Fiend mechanics. Does not increase XP gain.
- **Group scaling:** Solo-scaled, 2-player, 4-player, and 8-player public-event variants; HP scales by +65% per additional player after the first, damage scales by +8% per additional player, and loot eligibility requires active contribution.

**Raised monster stat block:**

### SEV-070 — Sonic-Scarred Incident: Echoing Redstone Gate

- **Required player level:** 26
- **Recommended combat rating:** 28
- **Event type:** Alliance Trial / Elite-Variant
- **XP reward:** 0 completion XP; 0 spawned-enemy XP
- **Trigger:** Trigger only when player level >= 26, player enters or completes a combat action inside Echoing Redstone Gate, and the sublocation has not awarded its weekly unique-loot eligibility. Completion XP and spawned-enemy XP are both forcibly set to 0.
- **Encounter goal:** Hunt the mobile flanker variant, protect isolated players from pin mechanics, and force the enemy into a punishable arena state.
- **Hazard profile:** elite spawn pressure, sublocation-specific chokepoints, and forced traversal interrupts
- **Empowered mechanic:** Sonic-Scarred Pack Latch: if the first latch is not broken within 4 seconds, a support hound joins and halves the victim’s healing received.
- **Failure state:** Event fails if the local anomaly reaches 100% intensity, all eligible players are downed, or the primary variant completes its empowered phase three times. Failure gives no XP and no loot roll.
- **Unique loot:** Echoing Iron-Jaw Ring — Epic Relic ring, item power 676
- **Loot rule:** Guaranteed first-clear: Echoing Iron-Jaw Ring pattern token + Epic Relic crafting imprint. Repeat clear: 16% chance for the unique ring; pity token after 8 eligible clears.

- **Group scaling:** Solo-scaled, 2-player, 4-player, and 8-player public-event variants; HP scales by +65% per additional player after the first, damage scales by +8% per additional player, and loot eligibility requires active contribution.

## The Scrap-Yard Labyrinth

### SEV-081 — Phase-Bound Incident: Magnetized Wall Maze
- **Sublocation:** Magnetized Wall Maze
- **Required player level:** 27
- **Recommended combat rating:** 29
- **Event type:** Elite Ambush / Elite-Variant
- **XP reward:** 0 completion XP; 0 spawned-enemy XP
- **Trigger:** Trigger only when player level >= 27, player enters or completes a combat action inside Magnetized Wall Maze, and the sublocation has not awarded its weekly unique-loot eligibility. Completion XP and spawned-enemy XP are both forcibly set to 0.
- **Encounter goal:** Control priority targets, solve the counter/vault pattern under added hazard pressure, and collapse the elite formation without dropping flow.
- **Hazard profile:** high-speed transit sweeps, lane swaps, and lethal timing windows
- **Empowered mechanic:** Phase-Bound Syncopation: Metronome Strike intentionally skips every fourth beat, punishing players who rely only on memorized rhythm.
- **Failure state:** Event fails if the local anomaly reaches 100% intensity, all eligible players are downed, or the primary variant completes its empowered phase three times. Failure gives no XP and no loot roll.
- **Unique loot:** Magnetized Tremor-Fiend Gauntlets — Epic Relic gauntlets, item power 666
- **Loot rule:** Guaranteed first-clear: Magnetized Tremor-Fiend Gauntlets pattern token + Epic Relic crafting imprint. Repeat clear: 16% chance for the unique gauntlets; pity token after 8 eligible clears.
- **Unique perk:** Unique Perk: while inside Scrap-Yard-type arenas, gain a short defensive or traversal proc after countering Tremor-Fiend mechanics. Does not increase XP gain.
- **Group scaling:** Solo-scaled, 2-player, 4-player, and 8-player public-event variants; HP scales by +65% per additional player after the first, damage scales by +8% per additional player, and loot eligibility requires active contribution.

- **Failure state:** Event fails if the local anomaly reaches 100% intensity, all eligible players are downed, or the primary variant completes its empowered phase three times. Failure gives no XP and no loot roll.
- **Unique loot:** Fire-Breathing Null Helmet — Epic Relic helmet, item power 709
- **Loot rule:** Guaranteed first-clear: Fire-Breathing Null Helmet pattern token + Epic Relic crafting imprint. Repeat clear: 16% chance for the unique helmet; pity token after 8 eligible clears.

### SEV-104 — Tide-Broken Incident: Mute Horizon Gate
- **Sublocation:** Mute Horizon Gate
- **Required player level:** 30
- **Recommended combat rating:** 32
- **Event type:** Timed Defense / Elite-Variant
- **XP reward:** 0 completion XP; 0 spawned-enemy XP
- **Trigger:** Trigger only when player level >= 30, player enters or completes a combat action inside Mute Horizon Gate, and the sublocation has not awarded its weekly unique-loot eligibility. Completion XP and spawned-enemy XP are both forcibly set to 0.
- **Encounter goal:** Survive a condensed horde pattern, prevent escalation loops, and eliminate the Nexus Swarmers variant commander before it converts the sublocation into a permanent hazard node.
- **Hazard profile:** tempo-locked shockwaves, parry-window distortion, and bass pulses that punish dropped combos
- **Empowered mechanic:** Tide-Broken Fusion Race: two surviving clusters can fuse after 24 seconds instead of 30, creating an over-shielded Nexus Warden.
- **Failure state:** Event fails if the local anomaly reaches 100% intensity, all eligible players are downed, or the primary variant completes its empowered phase three times. Failure gives no XP and no loot roll.
- **Unique loot:** Mute Nexus Back Trophy — Mythic Relic back trophy, item power 741
- **Loot rule:** Guaranteed first-clear: Mute Nexus Back Trophy pattern token + Mythic Relic crafting imprint. Repeat clear: 12% chance for the unique back trophy; pity token after 8 eligible clears.
- **Unique perk:** Unique Perk: while inside Phonetic-type arenas, gain a short defensive or traversal proc after countering Nexus Swarmers mechanics. Does not increase XP gain.
- **Group scaling:** Solo-scaled, 2-player, 4-player, and 8-player public-event variants; HP scales by +65% per additional player after the first, damage scales by +8% per additional player, and loot eligibility requires active contribution.

- **XP reward:** 0 completion XP; 0 spawned-enemy XP
- **Trigger:** Trigger only when player level >= 31, player enters or completes a combat action inside Elemental Cove, and the sublocation has not awarded its weekly unique-loot eligibility. Completion XP and spawned-enemy XP are both forcibly set to 0.
- **Encounter goal:** Defeat the raised Gnarl-Maws variant and cleanse the triggered anomaly without allowing the mechanic stack to reach maximum intensity.
- **Hazard profile:** pressure shifts, tidal knockback, and slow-motion parry timing
- **Empowered mechanic:** Grav-Torn Anchor Bite: latch effects stack movement slow and temporarily disable sprint cancels until shaken off with a heavy slam.
- **Failure state:** Event fails if the local anomaly reaches 100% intensity, all eligible players are downed, or the primary variant completes its empowered phase three times. Failure gives no XP and no loot roll.
- **Unique loot:** Elemental Gnarl-Maws Class Mod — Mythic Relic class mod, item power 766
- **Loot rule:** Guaranteed first-clear: Elemental Gnarl-Maws Class Mod pattern token + Mythic Relic crafting imprint. Repeat clear: 12% chance for the unique class mod; pity token after 8 eligible clears.
- **Unique perk:** Unique Perk: while inside Wayfora-type arenas, gain a short defensive or traversal proc after countering Gnarl-Maws mechanics. Does not increase XP gain.
- **Group scaling:** Solo-scaled, 2-player, 4-player, and 8-player public-event variants; HP scales by +65% per additional player after the first, damage scales by +8% per additional player, and loot eligibility requires active contribution.

## The Abyssal Trench

### SEV-116 — Ablative Incident: Cracked Glass Dome
- **Sublocation:** Cracked Glass Dome
- **Required player level:** 31
- **Recommended combat rating:** 33
- **Event type:** Horde Compression / Elite-Variant
- **XP reward:** 0 completion XP; 0 spawned-enemy XP
- **Trigger:** Trigger only when player level >= 31, player enters or completes a combat action inside Cracked Glass Dome, and the sublocation has not awarded its weekly unique-loot eligibility. Completion XP and spawned-enemy XP are both forcibly set to 0.
- **Encounter goal:** Survive a condensed horde pattern, prevent escalation loops, and eliminate the Tremor-Fiend variant commander before it converts the sublocation into a permanent hazard node.
- **Hazard profile:** high-speed transit sweeps, lane swaps, and lethal timing windows
- **Empowered mechanic:** Ablative Syncopation: Metronome Strike intentionally skips every fourth beat, punishing players who rely only on memorized rhythm.
- **Failure state:** Event fails if the local anomaly reaches 100% intensity, all eligible players are downed, or the primary variant completes its empowered phase three times. Failure gives no XP and no loot roll.
- **Unique loot:** Cracked Tremor-Fiend Mount Cosmetic — Mythic Relic mount cosmetic, item power 738
- **Loot rule:** Guaranteed first-clear: Cracked Tremor-Fiend Mount Cosmetic pattern token + Mythic Relic crafting imprint. Repeat clear: 12% chance for the unique mount cosmetic; pity token after 8 eligible clears.
- **Unique perk:** Unique Perk: while inside Abyssal-type arenas, gain a short defensive or traversal proc after countering Tremor-Fiend mechanics. Does not increase XP gain.
- **Group scaling:** Solo-scaled, 2-player, 4-player, and 8-player public-event variants; HP scales by +65% per additional player after the first, damage scales by +8% per additional player, and loot eligibility requires active contribution.

- **Hazard profile:** elite spawn pressure, sublocation-specific chokepoints, and forced traversal interrupts
- **Empowered mechanic:** Data-Forged Fusion Race: two surviving clusters can fuse after 24 seconds instead of 30, creating an over-shielded Nexus Warden.
- **Failure state:** Event fails if the local anomaly reaches 100% intensity, all eligible players are downed, or the primary variant completes its empowered phase three times. Failure gives no XP and no loot roll.
- **Unique loot:** Shareholder Nexus Amulet — Mythic Relic amulet, item power 806
- **Loot rule:** Guaranteed first-clear: Shareholder Nexus Amulet pattern token + Mythic Relic crafting imprint. Repeat clear: 12% chance for the unique amulet; pity token after 8 eligible clears.
- **Unique perk:** Unique Perk: while inside Syndicate-type arenas, gain a short defensive or traversal proc after countering Nexus Swarmers mechanics. Does not increase XP gain.
- **Group scaling:** Solo-scaled, 2-player, 4-player, and 8-player public-event variants; HP scales by +65% per additional player after the first, damage scales by +8% per additional player, and loot eligibility requires active contribution.

- **Encounter goal:** Break the Null Anomaly echo before its signature phase mechanic fully resolves, while suppressing support variants and maintaining encounter control.
- **Hazard profile:** elite spawn pressure, sublocation-specific chokepoints, and forced traversal interrupts
- **Empowered mechanic:** Spore-Sick Echo Rule: the boss repeats one signature world mechanic at 70%, 40%, and 15% health, each time with a tighter counter window.
- **Failure state:** Event fails if the local anomaly reaches 100% intensity, all eligible players are downed, or the primary variant completes its empowered phase three times. Failure gives no XP and no loot roll.

- **Loot rule:** Guaranteed first-clear: Cultivation Null Gauntlets pattern token + Ancient Relic crafting imprint. Repeat clear: 8% chance for the unique gauntlets; pity token after 8 eligible clears.

- **Group scaling:** Solo-scaled, 2-player, 4-player, and 8-player public-event variants; HP scales by +65% per additional player after the first, damage scales by +8% per additional player, and loot eligibility requires active contribution.

- **Recommended combat rating:** 42

- **Encounter goal:** Break the Astral Sovereign echo before its signature phase mechanic fully resolves, while suppressing support variants and maintaining encounter control.
- **Hazard profile:** gravity inversion, debris lanes, and delayed orbital strike telegraphs
- **Empowered mechanic:** Null-Branded Echo Rule: the boss repeats one signature world mechanic at 70%, 40%, and 15% health, each time with a tighter counter window.
- **Failure state:** Event fails if the local anomaly reaches 100% intensity, all eligible players are downed, or the primary variant completes its empowered phase three times. Failure gives no XP and no loot roll.
- **Unique loot:** Derelict Astral Back Trophy — Astral Artifact back trophy, item power 921
- **Loot rule:** Guaranteed first-clear: Derelict Astral Back Trophy pattern token + Astral Artifact crafting imprint. Repeat clear: 6% chance for the unique back trophy; pity token after 8 eligible clears.
- **Unique perk:** Unique Perk: while inside Lunar-type arenas, gain a short defensive or traversal proc after countering Astral Sovereign mechanics. Does not increase XP gain.
- **Group scaling:** Solo-scaled, 2-player, 4-player, and 8-player public-event variants; HP scales by +65% per additional player after the first, damage scales by +8% per additional player, and loot eligibility requires active contribution.

### SEV-207 — Ablative Incident: Unrendered Ledge Field
- **Sublocation:** Unrendered Ledge Field
- **Required player level:** 40
- **Recommended combat rating:** 42
- **Event type:** Mini-Boss Echo / Boss-Echo
- **XP reward:** 0 completion XP; 0 spawned-enemy XP
- **Trigger:** Trigger only when player level >= 40, player enters or completes a combat action inside Unrendered Ledge Field, and the sublocation has not awarded its weekly unique-loot eligibility. Completion XP and spawned-enemy XP are both forcibly set to 0.
- **Encounter goal:** Break the Null Anomaly echo before its signature phase mechanic fully resolves, while suppressing support variants and maintaining encounter control.
- **Hazard profile:** gravity inversion, debris lanes, and delayed orbital strike telegraphs
- **Empowered mechanic:** Ablative Echo Rule: the boss repeats one signature world mechanic at 70%, 40%, and 15% health, each time with a tighter counter window.
- **Failure state:** Event fails if the local anomaly reaches 100% intensity, all eligible players are downed, or the primary variant completes its empowered phase three times. Failure gives no XP and no loot roll.
- **Unique loot:** Unrendered Null Amulet — Astral Artifact amulet, item power 907
- **Loot rule:** Guaranteed first-clear: Unrendered Null Amulet pattern token + Astral Artifact crafting imprint. Repeat clear: 6% chance for the unique amulet; pity token after 8 eligible clears.
- **Unique perk:** Unique Perk: while inside Front-Matter-type arenas, gain a short defensive or traversal proc after countering Null Anomaly mechanics. Does not increase XP gain.
- **Group scaling:** Solo-scaled, 2-player, 4-player, and 8-player public-event variants; HP scales by +65% per additional player after the first, damage scales by +8% per additional player, and loot eligibility requires active contribution.
